         from flask import Flask, render_template, redirect, url_for, request
         import os
         
         app = Flask(__name__)
         app.config['SECRET_KEY'] = 'dev-secret-key'
         
         DATA_DIR = 'data'
         
         # Utility functions to read and write data files
         
         def read_auctions():
             auctions = []
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'auctions.txt')
             if os.path.exists(path):
                 with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) == 9:
                             auctions.append({
                                 'auction_id': int(parts[0]),
                                 'item_name': parts[1],
                                 'description': parts[2],
                                 'category': parts[3],
                                 'starting_bid': float(parts[4]),
                                 'current_bid': float(parts[5]),
                                 'end_time': parts[6],
                                 'status': parts[7],
                                 'image_url': parts[8]
                             })
             return auctions
         
         
         def save_auctions(auctions):
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'auctions.txt')
             with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for auction in auctions:
                     line = '|'.join([
                         str(auction['auction_id']),
                         auction['item_name'],
                         auction['description'],
                         auction['category'],
                         f"{auction['starting_bid']:.2f}",
                         f"{auction['current_bid']:.2f}",
                         auction['end_time'],
                         auction['status'],
                         auction['image_url']
                     ])
                     f.write(line + '\n')
         
         
         def read_categories():
             categories = []
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'categories.txt')
             if os.path.exists(path):
                 with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) == 4:
                             categories.append({
                                 'category_id': int(parts[0]),
                                 'category_name': parts[1],
                                 'description': parts[2],
                                 'item_count': int(parts[3])
                             })
             return categories
         
         
         def read_bids():
             bids = []
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'bids.txt')
             if os.path.exists(path):
                 with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) == 5:
                             bids.append({
                                 'bid_id': int(parts[0]),
                                 'auction_id': int(parts[1]),
                                 'bidder_name': parts[2],
                                 'bid_amount': float(parts[3]),
                                 'bid_timestamp': parts[4]
                             })
             return bids
         
         
         def save_bids(bids):
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'bids.txt')
             with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for bid in bids:
                     line = '|'.join([
                         str(bid['bid_id']),
                         str(bid['auction_id']),
                         bid['bidder_name'],
                         f"{bid['bid_amount']:.2f}",
                         bid['bid_timestamp']
                     ])
                     f.write(line + '\n')
         
         
         def read_winners():
             winners = []
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'winners.txt')
             if os.path.exists(path):
                 with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) == 6:
                             winners.append({
                                 'winner_id': int(parts[0]),
                                 'auction_id': int(parts[1]),
                                 'item_name': parts[2],
                                 'winner_name': parts[3],
                                 'winning_bid': float(parts[4]),
                                 'win_date': parts[5]
                             })
             return winners
         
         
         def read_bid_history():
             bid_history = []
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'bid_history.txt')
             if os.path.exists(path):
                 with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) == 6:
                             bid_history.append({
                                 'history_id': int(parts[0]),
                                 'auction_id': int(parts[1]),
                                 'auction_name': parts[2],
                                 'bidder_name': parts[3],
                                 'bid_amount': float(parts[4]),
                                 'bid_timestamp': parts[5]
                             })
             return bid_history
         
         
         def read_trending():
             trending = []
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'trending.txt')
             if os.path.exists(path):
                 with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) == 6:
                             trending.append({
                                 'auction_id': int(parts[0]),
                                 'item_name': parts[1],
                                 'bid_count': int(parts[2]),
                                 'current_bid': float(parts[3]),
                                 'trending_rank': int(parts[4]),
                                 'time_period': parts[5]
                             })
             return trending
         
         
         # Route implementations
         
         @app.route('/')
         def root_redirect():
             return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))
         
         
         @app.route('/dashboard')
         def dashboard():
             auctions = read_auctions()
             trending = read_trending()
         
             # featured_auctions: list of dict{auction_id: int, item_name: str, current_bid: float, end_time: str, image_url: str}
             # We define featured as top 5 auctions by current_bid descending and status active
             featured_auctions = [
                 {
                     'auction_id': auc['auction_id'],
                     'item_name': auc['item_name'],
                     'current_bid': auc['current_bid'],
                     'end_time': auc['end_time'],
                     'image_url': auc['image_url']
                 }
                 for auc in auctions if auc['status'] == 'Active'
             ]
             featured_auctions.sort(key=lambda x: x['current_bid'], reverse=True)
             featured_auctions = featured_auctions[:5]
         
             # trending_auctions: list of dict{auction_id: int, item_name: str, current_bid: float, bid_count: int, trending_rank: int}
             # Filter trending for a general period or latest, for simplicity take all times
             trending_auctions = [
                 {
                     'auction_id': t['auction_id'],
                     'item_name': t['item_name'],
                     'current_bid': t['current_bid'],
                     'bid_count': t['bid_count'],
                     'trending_rank': t['trending_rank']
                 }
                 for t in trending
             ]
         
             return render_template('dashboard.html', featured_auctions=featured_auctions, trending_auctions=trending_auctions)
         
         
         @app.route('/catalog')
         def auction_catalog():
             auctions = read_auctions()
             categories = read_categories()
         
             # auctions context list with all fields needed
             auctions_ctx = [
                 {
                     'auction_id': auc['auction_id'],
                     'item_name': auc['item_name'],
                     'description': auc['description'],
                     'category': auc['category'],
                     'current_bid': auc['current_bid'],
                     'end_time': auc['end_time'],
                     'image_url': auc['image_url']
                 }
                 for auc in auctions
             ]
         
             # categories list of strings for filter
             categories_list = [cat['category_name'] for cat in categories]
         
             return render_template('catalog.html', auctions=auctions_ctx, categories=categories_list)
         
         
         @app.route('/auction/<int:auction_id>')
         def auction_details(auction_id):
             auctions = read_auctions()
             bid_history = read_bid_history()
         
             auction = None
             for auc in auctions:
                 if auc['auction_id'] == auction_id:
                     auction = {
                         'auction_id': auc['auction_id'],
                         'item_name': auc['item_name'],
                         'description': auc['description'],
                         'current_bid': auc['current_bid'],
                         'end_time': auc['end_time'],
                         'status': auc['status'],
                         'image_url': auc['image_url']
                     }
                     break
         
             if auction is None:
                 return "Auction not found", 404
         
             bid_history_list = [
                 {
                     'bidder_name': bh['bidder_name'],
                     'bid_amount': bh['bid_amount'],
                     'bid_timestamp': bh['bid_timestamp']
                 }
                 for bh in bid_history if bh['auction_id'] == auction_id
             ]
         
             return render_template('auction_details.html', auction=auction, bid_history=bid_history_list)
         
         
         @app.route('/place_bid/<int:auction_id>')
         def place_bid(auction_id):
             auctions = read_auctions()
             auction = None
             for auc in auctions:
                 if auc['auction_id'] == auction_id:
                     auction = {
                         'auction_id': auc['auction_id'],
                         'item_name': auc['item_name'],
                         'minimum_bid': max(auc['current_bid'], auc['starting_bid'])
                     }
                     break
         
             if auction is None:
                 return "Auction not found", 404
         
             return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction)
         
         
         from datetime import datetime
         
         @app.route('/submit_bid/<int:auction_id>', methods=['POST'])
         def submit_bid(auction_id):
             bidder_name = request.form.get('bidder-name', '').strip()
             bid_amount_str = request.form.get('bid-amount', '').strip()
         
             # Validate inputs minimally
             if not bidder_name or not bid_amount_str:
                 error_msg = 'Bidder name and bid amount are required.'
                 auctions = read_auctions()
                 auction = None
                 for auc in auctions:
                     if auc['auction_id'] == auction_id:
                         auction = {
                             'auction_id': auc['auction_id'],
                             'item_name': auc['item_name'],
                             'minimum_bid': max(auc['current_bid'], auc['starting_bid'])
                         }
                         break
                 return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction, error=error_msg)
         
             try:
                 bid_amount = float(bid_amount_str)
             except ValueError:
                 error_msg = 'Bid amount must be a valid number.'
                 auctions = read_auctions()
                 auction = None
                 for auc in auctions:
                     if auc['auction_id'] == auction_id:
                         auction = {
                             'auction_id': auc['auction_id'],
                             'item_name': auc['item_name'],
                             'minimum_bid': max(auc['current_bid'], auc['starting_bid'])
                         }
                         break
                 return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction, error=error_msg)
         
             auctions = read_auctions()
             auction = None
             for auc in auctions:
                 if auc['auction_id'] == auction_id:
                     auction = auc
                     break
         
             if auction is None:
                 return "Auction not found", 404
         
             minimum_bid = max(auction['current_bid'], auction['starting_bid'])
             if bid_amount <= minimum_bid:
                 error_msg = f'Bid amount must be greater than current bid ({minimum_bid:.2f}).'
                 auction_ctx = {
                     'auction_id': auction['auction_id'],
                     'item_name': auction['item_name'],
                     'minimum_bid': minimum_bid
                 }
                 return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction_ctx, error=error_msg)
         
             # Add new bid
             bids = read_bids()
             next_bid_id = 1
             if bids:
                 next_bid_id = max(bid['bid_id'] for bid in bids) + 1
         
             now_str = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M')
         
             new_bid = {
                 'bid_id': next_bid_id,
                 'auction_id': auction_id,
                 'bidder_name': bidder_name,
                 'bid_amount': bid_amount,
                 'bid_timestamp': now_str
             }
             bids.append(new_bid)
             save_bids(bids)
         
             # Update auction current bid
             auction['current_bid'] = bid_amount
             save_auctions(auctions)
         
             # Also update bid_history.txt
             bid_history = read_bid_history()
             next_history_id = 1
             if bid_history:
                 next_history_id = max(bh['history_id'] for bh in bid_history) + 1
         
             new_bid_history = {
                 'history_id': next_history_id,
                 'auction_id': auction_id,
                 'auction_name': auction['item_name'],
                 'bidder_name': bidder_name,
                 'bid_amount': bid_amount,
                 'bid_timestamp': now_str
             }
             bid_history.append(new_bid_history)
             path_bid_hist = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'bid_history.txt')
             with open(path_bid_hist, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for bh in bid_history:
                     line = '|'.join([
                         str(bh['history_id']),
                         str(bh['auction_id']),
                         bh['auction_name'],
                         bh['bidder_name'],
                         f"{bh['bid_amount']:.2f}",
                         bh['bid_timestamp']
                     ])
                     f.write(line + '\n')
         
             return redirect(url_for('auction_details', auction_id=auction_id))
         
         
         @app.route('/bid_history')
         def bid_history():
             bids = read_bid_history()
             auctions = read_auctions()
         
             bids_ctx = [
                 {
                     'bid_id': bh['history_id'],
                     'auction_name': bh['auction_name'],
                     'bidder_name': bh['bidder_name'],
                     'bid_amount': bh['bid_amount'],
                     'bid_timestamp': bh['bid_timestamp']
                 }
                 for bh in bids
             ]
         
             auctions_ctx = [
                 {
                     'auction_id': auc['auction_id'],
                     'item_name': auc['item_name']
                 }
                 for auc in auctions
             ]
         
             return render_template('bid_history.html', bids=bids_ctx, auctions=auctions_ctx)
         
         
         @app.route('/categories')
         def auction_categories():
             categories = read_categories()
             return render_template('categories.html', categories=categories)
         
         
         @app.route('/category/<int:category_id>')
         def category_items(category_id):
             categories = read_categories()
             selected_category = None
             for cat in categories:
                 if cat['category_id'] == category_id:
                     selected_category = cat
                     break
         
             if selected_category is None:
                 return "Category not found", 404
         
             auctions = read_auctions()
             filtered_auctions = []
             for auc in auctions:
                 if auc['category'] == selected_category['category_name']:
                     filtered_auctions.append({
                         'auction_id': auc['auction_id'],
                         'item_name': auc['item_name'],
                         'description': auc['description'],
                         'category': auc['category'],
                         'current_bid': auc['current_bid'],
                         'end_time': auc['end_time'],
                         'image_url': auc['image_url']
                     })
         
             return render_template('catalog.html', auctions=filtered_auctions, categories=[cat['category_name'] for cat in categories])
         
         
         @app.route('/winners')
         def winners():
             winners = read_winners()
         
             winners_ctx = [
                 {
                     'winner_id': w['winner_id'],
                     'auction_id': w['auction_id'],
                     'item_name': w['item_name'],
                     'winner_name': w['winner_name'],
                     'winning_bid': w['winning_bid']
                 }
                 for w in winners
             ]
         
             return render_template('winners.html', winners=winners_ctx)
         
         
         @app.route('/trending')
         def trending_auctions():
             trending = read_trending()
         
             trending_auctions_ctx = [
                 {
                     'auction_id': t['auction_id'],
                     'item_name': t['item_name'],
                     'bid_count': t['bid_count'],
                     'current_bid': t['current_bid'],
                     'trending_rank': t['trending_rank'],
                     'time_period': t['time_period']
                 }
                 for t in trending
             ]
         
             return render_template('trending.html', trending_auctions=trending_auctions_ctx)
         
         
         @app.route('/auction_status')
         def auction_status():
             auctions = read_auctions()
         
             auctions_ctx = [
                 {
                     'auction_id': auc['auction_id'],
                     'item_name': auc['item_name'],
                     'status': auc['status'],
                     'end_time': auc['end_time'],
                     'current_bid': auc['current_bid']
                 }
                 for auc in auctions
             ]
         
             return render_template('auction_status.html', auctions=auctions_ctx)
         
         
         if __name__ == '__main__':
             app.run(debug=True, port=5000)

         from flask import Flask, render_template, redirect, url_for, request
         import os
         
         app = Flask(__name__)
         app.config['SECRET_KEY'] = 'dev-secret-key'
         
         DATA_DIR = 'data'
         
         # Utility functions to read and write data files
         
         def read_auctions():
             auctions = []
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'auctions.txt')
             if os.path.exists(path):
                 with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) == 9:
                             auctions.append({
                                 'auction_id': int(parts[0]),
                                 'item_name': parts[1],
                                 'description': parts[2],
                                 'category': parts[3],
                                 'starting_bid': float(parts[4]),
                                 'current_bid': float(parts[5]),
                                 'end_time': parts[6],
                                 'status': parts[7],
                                 'image_url': parts[8]
                             })
             return auctions
         
         
         def save_auctions(auctions):
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'auctions.txt')
             with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for auction in auctions:
                     line = '|'.join([
                         str(auction['auction_id']),
                         auction['item_name'],
                         auction['description'],
                         auction['category'],
                         f"{auction['starting_bid']:.2f}",
                         f"{auction['current_bid']:.2f}",
                         auction['end_time'],
                         auction['status'],
                         auction['image_url']
                     ])
                     f.write(line + '\n')
         
         
         def read_categories():
             categories = []
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'categories.txt')
             if os.path.exists(path):
                 with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) == 4:
                             categories.append({
                                 'category_id': int(parts[0]),
                                 'category_name': parts[1],
                                 'description': parts[2],
                                 'item_count': int(parts[3])
                             })
             return categories
         
         
         def read_bids():
             bids = []
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'bids.txt')
             if os.path.exists(path):
                 with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) == 5:
                             bids.append({
                                 'bid_id': int(parts[0]),
                                 'auction_id': int(parts[1]),
                                 'bidder_name': parts[2],
                                 'bid_amount': float(parts[3]),
                                 'bid_timestamp': parts[4]
                             })
             return bids
         
         
         def save_bids(bids):
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'bids.txt')
             with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for bid in bids:
                     line = '|'.join([
                         str(bid['bid_id']),
                         str(bid['auction_id']),
                         bid['bidder_name'],
                         f"{bid['bid_amount']:.2f}",
                         bid['bid_timestamp']
                     ])
                     f.write(line + '\n')
         
         
         def read_winners():
             winners = []
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'winners.txt')
             if os.path.exists(path):
                 with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) == 6:
                             winners.append({
                                 'winner_id': int(parts[0]),
                                 'auction_id': int(parts[1]),
                                 'item_name': parts[2],
                                 'winner_name': parts[3],
                                 'winning_bid': float(parts[4]),
                                 'win_date': parts[5]
                             })
             return winners
         
         
         def read_bid_history():
             bid_history = []
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'bid_history.txt')
             if os.path.exists(path):
                 with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) == 6:
                             bid_history.append({
                                 'history_id': int(parts[0]),
                                 'auction_id': int(parts[1]),
                                 'auction_name': parts[2],
                                 'bidder_name': parts[3],
                                 'bid_amount': float(parts[4]),
                                 'bid_timestamp': parts[5]
                             })
             return bid_history
         
         
         def read_trending():
             trending = []
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'trending.txt')
             if os.path.exists(path):
                 with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) == 6:
                             trending.append({
                                 'auction_id': int(parts[0]),
                                 'item_name': parts[1],
                                 'bid_count': int(parts[2]),
                                 'current_bid': float(parts[3]),
                                 'trending_rank': int(parts[4]),
                                 'time_period': parts[5]
                             })
             return trending
         
         
         # Route implementations
         
         @app.route('/')
         def root_redirect():
             return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))
         
         
         @app.route('/dashboard')
         def dashboard():
             auctions = read_auctions()
             trending = read_trending()
         
             # featured_auctions: list of dict{auction_id: int, item_name: str, current_bid: float, end_time: str, image_url: str}
             # We define featured as top 5 auctions by current_bid descending and status active
             featured_auctions = [
                 {
                     'auction_id': auc['auction_id'],
                     'item_name': auc['item_name'],
                     'current_bid': auc['current_bid'],
                     'end_time': auc['end_time'],
                     'image_url': auc['image_url']
                 }
                 for auc in auctions if auc['status'] == 'Active'
             ]
             featured_auctions.sort(key=lambda x: x['current_bid'], reverse=True)
             featured_auctions = featured_auctions[:5]
         
             # trending_auctions: list of dict{auction_id: int, item_name: str, current_bid: float, bid_count: int, trending_rank: int}
             # Filter trending for a general period or latest, for simplicity take all times
             trending_auctions = [
                 {
                     'auction_id': t['auction_id'],
                     'item_name': t['item_name'],
                     'current_bid': t['current_bid'],
                     'bid_count': t['bid_count'],
                     'trending_rank': t['trending_rank']
                 }
                 for t in trending
             ]
         
             return render_template('dashboard.html', featured_auctions=featured_auctions, trending_auctions=trending_auctions)
         
         
         @app.route('/catalog')
         def auction_catalog():
             auctions = read_auctions()
             categories = read_categories()
         
             # auctions context list with all fields needed
             auctions_ctx = [
                 {
                     'auction_id': auc['auction_id'],
                     'item_name': auc['item_name'],
                     'description': auc['description'],
                     'category': auc['category'],
                     'current_bid': auc['current_bid'],
                     'end_time': auc['end_time'],
                     'image_url': auc['image_url']
                 }
                 for auc in auctions
             ]
         
             # categories list of strings for filter
             categories_list = [cat['category_name'] for cat in categories]
         
             return render_template('catalog.html', auctions=auctions_ctx, categories=categories_list)
         
         
         @app.route('/auction/<int:auction_id>')
         def auction_details(auction_id):
             auctions = read_auctions()
             bid_history = read_bid_history()
         
             auction = None
             for auc in auctions:
                 if auc['auction_id'] == auction_id:
                     auction = {
                         'auction_id': auc['auction_id'],
                         'item_name': auc['item_name'],
                         'description': auc['description'],
                         'current_bid': auc['current_bid'],
                         'end_time': auc['end_time'],
                         'status': auc['status'],
                         'image_url': auc['image_url']
                     }
                     break
         
             if auction is None:
                 return "Auction not found", 404
         
             bid_history_list = [
                 {
                     'bidder_name': bh['bidder_name'],
                     'bid_amount': bh['bid_amount'],
                     'bid_timestamp': bh['bid_timestamp']
                 }
                 for bh in bid_history if bh['auction_id'] == auction_id
             ]
         
             return render_template('auction_details.html', auction=auction, bid_history=bid_history_list)
         
         
         @app.route('/place_bid/<int:auction_id>')
         def place_bid(auction_id):
             auctions = read_auctions()
             auction = None
             for auc in auctions:
                 if auc['auction_id'] == auction_id:
                     auction = {
                         'auction_id': auc['auction_id'],
                         'item_name': auc['item_name'],
                         'minimum_bid': max(auc['current_bid'], auc['starting_bid'])
                     }
                     break
         
             if auction is None:
                 return "Auction not found", 404
         
             return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction)
         
         
         from datetime import datetime
         
         @app.route('/submit_bid/<int:auction_id>', methods=['POST'])
         def submit_bid(auction_id):
             bidder_name = request.form.get('bidder-name', '').strip()
             bid_amount_str = request.form.get('bid-amount', '').strip()
         
             # Validate inputs minimally
             if not bidder_name or not bid_amount_str:
                 error_msg = 'Bidder name and bid amount are required.'
                 auctions = read_auctions()
                 auction = None
                 for auc in auctions:
                     if auc['auction_id'] == auction_id:
                         auction = {
                             'auction_id': auc['auction_id'],
                             'item_name': auc['item_name'],
                             'minimum_bid': max(auc['current_bid'], auc['starting_bid'])
                         }
                         break
                 return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction, error=error_msg)
         
             try:
                 bid_amount = float(bid_amount_str)
             except ValueError:
                 error_msg = 'Bid amount must be a valid number.'
                 auctions = read_auctions()
                 auction = None
                 for auc in auctions:
                     if auc['auction_id'] == auction_id:
                         auction = {
                             'auction_id': auc['auction_id'],
                             'item_name': auc['item_name'],
                             'minimum_bid': max(auc['current_bid'], auc['starting_bid'])
                         }
                         break
                 return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction, error=error_msg)
         
             auctions = read_auctions()
             auction = None
             for auc in auctions:
                 if auc['auction_id'] == auction_id:
                     auction = auc
                     break
         
             if auction is None:
                 return "Auction not found", 404
         
             minimum_bid = max(auction['current_bid'], auction['starting_bid'])
             if bid_amount <= minimum_bid:
                 error_msg = f'Bid amount must be greater than current bid ({minimum_bid:.2f}).'
                 auction_ctx = {
                     'auction_id': auction['auction_id'],
                     'item_name': auction['item_name'],
                     'minimum_bid': minimum_bid
                 }
                 return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction_ctx, error=error_msg)
         
             # Add new bid
             bids = read_bids()
             next_bid_id = 1
             if bids:
                 next_bid_id = max(bid['bid_id'] for bid in bids) + 1
         
             now_str = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M')
         
             new_bid = {
                 'bid_id': next_bid_id,
                 'auction_id': auction_id,
                 'bidder_name': bidder_name,
                 'bid_amount': bid_amount,
                 'bid_timestamp': now_str
             }
             bids.append(new_bid)
             save_bids(bids)
         
             # Update auction current bid
             auction['current_bid'] = bid_amount
             save_auctions(auctions)
         
             # Also update bid_history.txt
             bid_history = read_bid_history()
             next_history_id = 1
             if bid_history:
                 next_history_id = max(bh['history_id'] for bh in bid_history) + 1
         
             new_bid_history = {
                 'history_id': next_history_id,
                 'auction_id': auction_id,
                 'auction_name': auction['item_name'],
                 'bidder_name': bidder_name,
                 'bid_amount': bid_amount,
                 'bid_timestamp': now_str
             }
             bid_history.append(new_bid_history)
             path_bid_hist = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'bid_history.txt')
             with open(path_bid_hist, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for bh in bid_history:
                     line = '|'.join([
                         str(bh['history_id']),
                         str(bh['auction_id']),
                         bh['auction_name'],
                         bh['bidder_name'],
                         f"{bh['bid_amount']:.2f}",
                         bh['bid_timestamp']
                     ])
                     f.write(line + '\n')
         
             return redirect(url_for('auction_details', auction_id=auction_id))
         
         
         @app.route('/bid_history')
         def bid_history():
             bids = read_bid_history()
             auctions = read_auctions()
         
             bids_ctx = [
                 {
                     'bid_id': bh['history_id'],
                     'auction_name': bh['auction_name'],
                     'bidder_name': bh['bidder_name'],
                     'bid_amount': bh['bid_amount'],
                     'bid_timestamp': bh['bid_timestamp']
                 }
                 for bh in bids
             ]
         
             auctions_ctx = [
                 {
                     'auction_id': auc['auction_id'],
                     'item_name': auc['item_name']
                 }
                 for auc in auctions
             ]
         
             return render_template('bid_history.html', bids=bids_ctx, auctions=auctions_ctx)
         
         
         @app.route('/categories')
         def auction_categories():
             categories = read_categories()
             return render_template('categories.html', categories=categories)
         
         
         @app.route('/category/<int:category_id>')
         def category_items(category_id):
             categories = read_categories()
             selected_category = None
             for cat in categories:
                 if cat['category_id'] == category_id:
                     selected_category = cat
                     break
         
             if selected_category is None:
                 return "Category not found", 404
         
             auctions = read_auctions()
             filtered_auctions = []
             for auc in auctions:
                 if auc['category'] == selected_category['category_name']:
                     filtered_auctions.append({
                         'auction_id': auc['auction_id'],
                         'item_name': auc['item_name'],
                         'description': auc['description'],
                         'category': auc['category'],
                         'current_bid': auc['current_bid'],
                         'end_time': auc['end_time'],
                         'image_url': auc['image_url']
                     })
         
             return render_template('catalog.html', auctions=filtered_auctions, categories=[cat['category_name'] for cat in categories])
         
         
         @app.route('/winners')
         def winners():
             winners = read_winners()
         
             winners_ctx = [
                 {
                     'winner_id': w['winner_id'],
                     'auction_id': w['auction_id'],
                     'item_name': w['item_name'],
                     'winner_name': w['winner_name'],
                     'winning_bid': w['winning_bid']
                 }
                 for w in winners
             ]
         
             return render_template('winners.html', winners=winners_ctx)
         
         
         @app.route('/trending')
         def trending_auctions():
             trending = read_trending()
         
             trending_auctions_ctx = [
                 {
                     'auction_id': t['auction_id'],

             ]

         @app.route('/auction_status')
         def auction_status():
             auctions = read_auctions()
         
             auctions_ctx = [
                 {
                     'auction_id': auc['auction_id'],
                     'item_name': auc['item_name'],
                     'status': auc['status'],
                     'end_time': auc['end_time'],
                     'current_bid': auc['current_bid']
                 }
                 for auc in auctions
             ]
         
             return render_template('auction_status.html', auctions=auctions_ctx)

         from flask import Flask, render_template, redirect, url_for, request
         import os
         
         app = Flask(__name__)
         app.config['SECRET_KEY'] = 'dev-secret-key'
         
         DATA_DIR = 'data'
         
         # Utility functions to read and write data files
         
         def read_auctions():
             auctions = []
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'auctions.txt')
             if os.path.exists(path):
                 with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) == 9:
                             auctions.append({
                                 'auction_id': int(parts[0]),
                                 'item_name': parts[1],
                                 'description': parts[2],
                                 'category': parts[3],
                                 'starting_bid': float(parts[4]),
                                 'current_bid': float(parts[5]),
                                 'end_time': parts[6],
                                 'status': parts[7],
                                 'image_url': parts[8]
                             })
             return auctions
         
         
         def save_auctions(auctions):
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'auctions.txt')
             with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for auction in auctions:
                     line = '|'.join([
                         str(auction['auction_id']),
                         auction['item_name'],
                         auction['description'],
                         auction['category'],
                         f"{auction['starting_bid']:.2f}",
                         f"{auction['current_bid']:.2f}",
                         auction['end_time'],
                         auction['status'],
                         auction['image_url']
                     ])
                     f.write(line + '\n')
         
         
         def read_categories():
             categories = []
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'categories.txt')
             if os.path.exists(path):
                 with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) == 4:
                             categories.append({
                                 'category_id': int(parts[0]),
                                 'category_name': parts[1],
                                 'description': parts[2],
                                 'item_count': int(parts[3])
                             })
             return categories
         
         
         def read_bids():
             bids = []
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'bids.txt')
             if os.path.exists(path):
                 with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) == 5:
                             bids.append({
                                 'bid_id': int(parts[0]),
                                 'auction_id': int(parts[1]),
                                 'bidder_name': parts[2],
                                 'bid_amount': float(parts[3]),
                                 'bid_timestamp': parts[4]
                             })
             return bids
         
         
         def save_bids(bids):
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'bids.txt')
             with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for bid in bids:
                     line = '|'.join([
                         str(bid['bid_id']),
                         str(bid['auction_id']),
                         bid['bidder_name'],
                         f"{bid['bid_amount']:.2f}",
                         bid['bid_timestamp']
                     ])
                     f.write(line + '\n')
         
         
         def read_winners():
             winners = []
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'winners.txt')
             if os.path.exists(path):
                 with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) == 6:
                             winners.append({
                                 'winner_id': int(parts[0]),
                                 'auction_id': int(parts[1]),
                                 'item_name': parts[2],
                                 'winner_name': parts[3],
                                 'winning_bid': float(parts[4]),
                                 'win_date': parts[5]
                             })
             return winners
         
         
         def read_bid_history():
             bid_history = []
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'bid_history.txt')
             if os.path.exists(path):
                 with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) == 6:
                             bid_history.append({
                                 'history_id': int(parts[0]),
                                 'auction_id': int(parts[1]),
                                 'auction_name': parts[2],
                                 'bidder_name': parts[3],
                                 'bid_amount': float(parts[4]),
                                 'bid_timestamp': parts[5]
                             })
             return bid_history
         
         
         def read_trending():
             trending = []
             path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'trending.txt')
             if os.path.exists(path):
                 with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) == 6:
                             trending.append({
                                 'auction_id': int(parts[0]),
                                 'item_name': parts[1],
                                 'bid_count': int(parts[2]),
                                 'current_bid': float(parts[3]),
                                 'trending_rank': int(parts[4]),
                                 'time_period': parts[5]
                             })
             return trending
         
         
         # Route implementations
         
         @app.route('/')
         def root_redirect():
             return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))
         
         
         @app.route('/dashboard')
         def dashboard():
             auctions = read_auctions()
             trending = read_trending()
         
             # featured_auctions: list of dict{auction_id: int, item_name: str, current_bid: float, end_time: str, image_url: str}
             # We define featured as top 5 auctions by current_bid descending and status active
             featured_auctions = [
                 {
                     'auction_id': auc['auction_id'],
                     'item_name': auc['item_name'],
                     'current_bid': auc['current_bid'],
                     'end_time': auc['end_time'],
                     'image_url': auc['image_url']
                 }
                 for auc in auctions if auc['status'] == 'Active'
             ]
             featured_auctions.sort(key=lambda x: x['current_bid'], reverse=True)
             featured_auctions = featured_auctions[:5]
         
             # trending_auctions: list of dict{auction_id: int, item_name: str, current_bid: float, bid_count: int, trending_rank: int}
             # Filter trending for a general period or latest, for simplicity take all times
             trending_auctions = [
                 {
                     'auction_id': t['auction_id'],
                     'item_name': t['item_name'],
                     'current_bid': t['current_bid'],
                     'bid_count': t['bid_count'],
                     'trending_rank': t['trending_rank']
                 }
                 for t in trending
             ]
         
             return render_template('dashboard.html', featured_auctions=featured_auctions, trending_auctions=trending_auctions)
         
         
         @app.route('/catalog')
         def auction_catalog():
             auctions = read_auctions()
             categories = read_categories()
         
             # auctions context list with all fields needed
             auctions_ctx = [
                 {
                     'auction_id': auc['auction_id'],
                     'item_name': auc['item_name'],
                     'description': auc['description'],
                     'category': auc['category'],
                     'current_bid': auc['current_bid'],
                     'end_time': auc['end_time'],
                     'image_url': auc['image_url']
                 }
                 for auc in auctions
             ]
         
             # categories list of strings for filter
             categories_list = [cat['category_name'] for cat in categories]
         
             return render_template('catalog.html', auctions=auctions_ctx, categories=categories_list)
         
         
         @app.route('/auction/<int:auction_id>')
         def auction_details(auction_id):
             auctions = read_auctions()
             bid_history = read_bid_history()
         
             auction = None
             for auc in auctions:
                 if auc['auction_id'] == auction_id:
                     auction = {
                         'auction_id': auc['auction_id'],
                         'item_name': auc['item_name'],
                         'description': auc['description'],
                         'current_bid': auc['current_bid'],
                         'end_time': auc['end_time'],
                         'status': auc['status'],
                         'image_url': auc['image_url']
                     }
                     break
         
             if auction is None:
                 return "Auction not found", 404
         
             bid_history_list = [
                 {
                     'bidder_name': bh['bidder_name'],
                     'bid_amount': bh['bid_amount'],
                     'bid_timestamp': bh['bid_timestamp']
                 }
                 for bh in bid_history if bh['auction_id'] == auction_id
             ]
         
             return render_template('auction_details.html', auction=auction, bid_history=bid_history_list)
         
         
         @app.route('/place_bid/<int:auction_id>')
         def place_bid(auction_id):
             auctions = read_auctions()
             auction = None
             for auc in auctions:
                 if auc['auction_id'] == auction_id:
                     auction = {
                         'auction_id': auc['auction_id'],
                         'item_name': auc['item_name'],
                         'minimum_bid': max(auc['current_bid'], auc['starting_bid'])
                     }
                     break
         
             if auction is None:
                 return "Auction not found", 404
         
             return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction)
         
         
         from datetime import datetime
         
         @app.route('/submit_bid/<int:auction_id>', methods=['POST'])
         def submit_bid(auction_id):
             bidder_name = request.form.get('bidder-name', '').strip()
             bid_amount_str = request.form.get('bid-amount', '').strip()
         
             # Validate inputs minimally
             if not bidder_name or not bid_amount_str:
                 error_msg = 'Bidder name and bid amount are required.'
                 auctions = read_auctions()
                 auction = None
                 for auc in auctions:
                     if auc['auction_id'] == auction_id:
                         auction = {
                             'auction_id': auc['auction_id'],
                             'item_name': auc['item_name'],
                             'minimum_bid': max(auc['current_bid'], auc['starting_bid'])
                         }
                         break
                 return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction, error=error_msg)
         
             try:
                 bid_amount = float(bid_amount_str)
             except ValueError:
                 error_msg = 'Bid amount must be a valid number.'
                 auctions = read_auctions()
                 auction = None
                 for auc in auctions:
                     if auc['auction_id'] == auction_id:
                         auction = {
                             'auction_id': auc['auction_id'],
                             'item_name': auc['item_name'],
                             'minimum_bid': max(auc['current_bid'], auc['starting_bid'])
                         }
                         break
                 return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction, error=error_msg)
         
             auctions = read_auctions()
             auction = None
             for auc in auctions:
                 if auc['auction_id'] == auction_id:
                     auction = auc
                     break
         
             if auction is None:
                 return "Auction not found", 404
         
             minimum_bid = max(auction['current_bid'], auction['starting_bid'])
             if bid_amount <= minimum_bid:
                 error_msg = f'Bid amount must be greater than current bid ({minimum_bid:.2f}).'
                 auction_ctx = {
                     'auction_id': auction['auction_id'],
                     'item_name': auction['item_name'],
                     'minimum_bid': minimum_bid
                 }
                 return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction_ctx, error=error_msg)
         
             # Add new bid
             bids = read_bids()
             next_bid_id = 1
             if bids:
                 next_bid_id = max(bid['bid_id'] for bid in bids) + 1
         
             now_str = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M')
         
             new_bid = {
                 'bid_id': next_bid_id,
                 'auction_id': auction_id,
                 'bidder_name': bidder_name,
                 'bid_amount': bid_amount,
                 'bid_timestamp': now_str
             }
             bids.append(new_bid)
             save_bids(bids)
         
             # Update auction current bid
             auction['current_bid'] = bid_amount
             save_auctions(auctions)
         
             # Also update bid_history.txt
             bid_history = read_bid_history()
             next_history_id = 1
             if bid_history:
                 next_history_id = max(bh['history_id'] for bh in bid_history) + 1
         
             new_bid_history = {
                 'history_id': next_history_id,
                 'auction_id': auction_id,
                 'auction_name': auction['item_name'],
                 'bidder_name': bidder_name,
                 'bid_amount': bid_amount,
                 'bid_timestamp': now_str
             }
             bid_history.append(new_bid_history)
             path_bid_hist = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'bid_history.txt')
             with open(path_bid_hist, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for bh in bid_history:
                     line = '|'.join([
                         str(bh['history_id']),
                         str(bh['auction_id']),
                         bh['auction_name'],
                         bh['bidder_name'],
                         f"{bh['bid_amount']:.2f}",
                         bh['bid_timestamp']
                     ])
                     f.write(line + '\n')
         
             return redirect(url_for('auction_details', auction_id=auction_id))
         
         
         @app.route('/bid_history')
         def bid_history():
             bids = read_bid_history()
             auctions = read_auctions()
         
             bids_ctx = [
                 {
                     'bid_id': bh['history_id'],
                     'auction_name': bh['auction_name'],
                     'bidder_name': bh['bidder_name'],
                     'bid_amount': bh['bid_amount'],
                     'bid_timestamp': bh['bid_timestamp']
                 }
                 for bh in bids
             ]
         
             auctions_ctx = [
                 {
                     'auction_id': auc['auction_id'],
                     'item_name': auc['item_name']
                 }
                 for auc in auctions
             ]
         
             return render_template('bid_history.html', bids=bids_ctx, auctions=auctions_ctx)
         
         
         @app.route('/categories')
         def auction_categories():
             categories = read_categories()
             return render_template('categories.html', categories=categories)
         
         
         @app.route('/category/<int:category_id>')
         def category_items(category_id):
             categories = read_categories()
             selected_category = None
             for cat in categories:
                 if cat['category_id'] == category_id:
                     selected_category = cat
                     break
         
             if selected_category is None:
                 return "Category not found", 404
         
             auctions = read_auctions()
             filtered_auctions = []
             for auc in auctions:
                 if auc['category'] == selected_category['category_name']:
                     filtered_auctions.append({
                         'auction_id': auc['auction_id'],
                         'item_name': auc['item_name'],
                         'description': auc['description'],
                         'category': auc['category'],
                         'current_bid': auc['current_bid'],
                         'end_time': auc['end_time'],
                         'image_url': auc['image_url']
                     })
         
             return render_template('catalog.html', auctions=filtered_auctions, categories=[cat['category_name'] for cat in categories])
         
         
         @app.route('/winners')
         def winners():
             winners = read_winners()
         
             winners_ctx = [
                 {
                     'winner_id': w['winner_id'],
                     'auction_id': w['auction_id'],
                     'item_name': w['item_name'],
                     'winner_name': w['winner_name'],
                     'winning_bid': w['winning_bid']
                 }
                 for w in winners
             ]
         
             return render_template('winners.html', winners=winners_ctx)
         
         
         @app.route('/trending')
         def trending_auctions():
             trending = read_trending()
         
             trending_auctions_ctx = [
                 {
                     'auction_id': t['auction_id'],
                     'item_name': t['item_name'],
                     'bid_count': t['bid_count'],
                     'current_bid': t['current_bid'],
                     'trending_rank': t['trending_rank'],
                     'time_period': t['time_period']
                 }
                 for t in trending
             ]
         
             return render_template('trending.html', trending_auctions=trending_auctions_ctx)
         
         
         @app.route('/auction_status')
         def auction_status():
             auctions = read_auctions()
         
             auctions_ctx = [
                 {
                     'auction_id': auc['auction_id'],
                     'item_name': auc['item_name'],
                     'status': auc['status'],
                     'end_time': auc['end_time'],
                     'current_bid': auc['current_bid']
                 }
                 for auc in auctions
             ]
         
             return render_template('auction_status.html', auctions=auctions_ctx)

         Retest backend app.py and generate backend_feedback.txt
         === app.py ===
         from flask import Flask, render_template, request, jsonify
         import os
         
         app = Flask(__name__)
         
         DATA_FOLDER = os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), 'data')
         
         
         # Utility functions to load data from files
         
         def load_users():
             users = []
             try:
                 with open(os.path.join(DATA_FOLDER, 'users.txt'), 'r') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split(',')
                         if len(parts) == 3:
                             users.append({
                                 'username': parts[0],
                                 'password': parts[1],
                                 'email': parts[2]
                             })
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return users
         
         
         def load_categories():
             categories = []
             try:
                 with open(os.path.join(DATA_FOLDER, 'categories.txt'), 'r') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         categories.append(line.strip())
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return categories
         
         
         def load_auctions():
             auctions = []
             try:
                 with open(os.path.join(DATA_FOLDER, 'auctions.txt'), 'r') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split(',')
                         # Assuming auctions.txt line format: id,product_name,category,starting_price,current_price,seller,bid_count
                         if len(parts) == 7:
                             auctions.append({
                                 'id': parts[0],
                                 'product_name': parts[1],
                                 'category': parts[2],
                                 'starting_price': float(parts[3]),
                                 'current_price': float(parts[4]),
                                 'seller': parts[5],
                                 'bid_count': int(parts[6])
                             })
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return auctions
         
         
         @app.route('/')
         def home():
             categories = load_categories()
             auctions = load_auctions()
             return render_template('home.html', categories=categories, auctions=auctions)
         
         
         @app.route('/auctions')
         def auctions():
             auctions = load_auctions()
             return jsonify(auctions)
         
         
         @app.route('/users')
         def users():
             users = load_users()
             return jsonify(users)
         
         
         if __name__ == '__main__':
             app.run(debug=True)

                                 'product_name': parts[1],
                                 'category': parts[2],
                                 'starting_price': float(parts[3]),
                                 'current_price': float(parts[4]),
                                 'seller': parts[5],
                                 'bid_count': int(parts[6])
                             })
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return auctions
         
         
         @app.route('/')
         def home():
             categories = load_categories()
             auctions = load_auctions()
             return render_template('home.html', categories=categories, auctions=auctions)
         
         
         @app.route('/auctions')
         def auctions():
             auctions = load_auctions()
             return jsonify(auctions)
         
         
         @app.route('/users')
         def users():
             users = load_users()
             return jsonify(users)
         
         
         if __name__ == '__main__':
             app.run(debug=True)
